<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I _ {\mathrm {B}} = (1 - \alpha) I _ {\mathrm {E}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; <p>This is shown in Fig. 2.10 (c).</p>
<p>(2.3)</p>
<p>(2) Current Gain of Transistor in Common-Emitter Configuration</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251223-7402dd88.jpeg" alt="img-20.jpeg">
(a) Common-emitter NPN transistor circuit.</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251223-b57aa0c2.jpeg" alt="img-21.jpeg">
(b) Common-emitter PNP transistor circuit.
Figure 2.11 Common emitter configuration</p>
<p>Consider a transistor (either NPN or PNP) connected in a common-emitter configuration as shown in Fig. 2.11 (a) and (b). Here, the base current is the input current and the collector current is the output current. The ratio of collector current to base current is called current gain  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>β</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\beta)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>  of the transistor. Since the base current and collector current may be direct or alternating current, therefore we define</p>
<p>Transistors</p>
<p>two types of current gains namely d.c. current gain and a.c. current gain.</p>
<p>(a) Common-emitter d.c. current gain <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>β</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\beta)_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2806em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> It is defined as the ratio of collector current <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(I_C)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> to corresponding base current <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>B</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(I_B)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> and is designated by <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span>, or <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>β</mi><mrow><mi>d</mi><mi>c</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta_{dc}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> or <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mrow><mi>F</mi><mi>E</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_{FE}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">FE</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. Mathematically, the common-emitter d.c. current gain is given by the relation,</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable width="100%"><mtr><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mrow><mi>β</mi><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>B</mi></msub></mrow></mtd><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mtext>(2.4)</mtext></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta = I_C / I_B \tag{2.4}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="tag"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2.4</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>or</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mi>β</mi><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>B</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I_C = \beta I_B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>Since collector current of a transistor is much larger than the base current, the value of <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span> is much greater than unity. Typical values of <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span> may range from 20 to 250. It is also called common-emitter dc forward transfer ratio and is written as <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mrow><mi>F</mi><mi>E</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_{FE}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">FE</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. It is possible for <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span> to have as high a value as 500.</p>
<p>(b) Common emitter a.c. current gain <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>β</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\beta_0)_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2806em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> It is defined as the ratio of small change in collector current <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\Delta I_C)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> to the corresponding small change in base current <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>B</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\Delta I_B)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> for a constant collector-to-emitter voltage <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>E</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(V_{CE})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">CE</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>. It is designated by <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>β</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> or <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>β</mi><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta_{ac}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. Mathematically common-emitter a.c. current gain is given by the relation,</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable width="100%"><mtr><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mrow><msub><mi>β</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>B</mi></msub></mrow></mtd><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mtext>(2.5)</mtext></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta_0 = \Delta I_C / \Delta I_B \tag{2.5}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/Δ</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="tag"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2.5</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>The term <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>β</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is also called common-emitter short circuit current gain or small-signal common-emitter current gain. It is interesting to know that <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>β</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> or <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mrow><mi>f</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_{fe}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9805em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is a parameter used in the analysis of small-signal transistor amplifier circuits. <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>β</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> have a range of values similar to that mentioned for <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span>. For all practical purposes, d.c. current gain and a.c. current gain are considered to be equal. i.e. <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>β</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta = \beta_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0528em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="c0ec3a54">Relationship between <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span>:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#c0ec3a54" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>We know that emitter current <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>E</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(I_E)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; <p>Dividing the above equation on both sides by <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I_C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>,</p>

<p>Since</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mfrac><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>E</mi></msub><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mi>α</mi><mtext>&nbsp;and&nbsp;</mtext><mfrac><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>B</mi></msub><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>C</mi></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mi>β</mi><mtext>&nbsp;then&nbsp;</mtext><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>α</mi></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>β</mi></mfrac><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow><mi>β</mi></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac{I_E}{I_C} = \alpha \text{ and } \frac{I_B}{I_C} = \beta \text{ then } \frac{1}{\alpha} = \frac{1}{\beta} + 1 = \frac{1 + \beta}{\beta}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.1963em; <div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable width="100%"><mtr><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mrow><mo>∴</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>α</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mi>β</mi><mrow><mi>β</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mfrac></mrow></mtd><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mtext>(2.6)</mtext></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\therefore \quad \alpha = \frac{\beta}{\beta + 1} \tag{2.6}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">∴</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.2519em; <p>The above expression may be written as</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>β</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha (\beta + 1) = \beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>β</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>α</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha . \beta + \alpha = \beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>β</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>α</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>β</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>β</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha = \beta - \alpha . \beta = \beta (1 - \alpha)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; <p>or</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mi>α</mi><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow></mfrac><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo>…</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2.7</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta = \frac {\alpha}{1 - \alpha} \quad \dots (2. 7)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; <p>Also using above eqns., we can deduce:</p>

(iii)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></msub><mi>α</mi></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow><mi>β</mi></mfrac><mo>⋅</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>β</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I_{\mathrm{E}} = \frac{I_{\mathrm{C}}}{\alpha} = \frac{1 + \beta}{\beta} \cdot I_{\mathrm{C}} = (1 + \beta) I_{\mathrm{B}} = \frac{I_{\mathrm{B}}}{(1 - \alpha)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; (iv) The three transistor dc currents always bear the following ratio</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub><mo>:</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></msub><mo>:</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></msub><mo>:</mo><mo>:</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>:</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>:</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I _ {\mathrm {E}}: I _ {\mathrm {B}}: I _ {\mathrm {C}}:: 1: (1 - \alpha): \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; <p>(3) Current Gain of a Transistor in Common-Collector Configuration:</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251223-e7596f93.jpeg" alt="img-22.jpeg">
(a) Common-collector NPN transistor circuit.
Figure 2.12 Common collector configuration</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251223-090dcf90.jpeg" alt="img-23.jpeg">
(b) Common-collector PNP transistor circuit.</p>
<p>Fig. 2.12 (a) and (b) show a NPN and PNP transistor connected in a common-collector configuration respectively. The voltages  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{V_{BB}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0139em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">BB</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  forward-biases the emitter-base junction, and  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{V_{CC}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0139em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">CC</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  reverse-biases the collector-base junction of the transistor. Here, the collector is not at d.c. ground. But it is at a.c. ground. It is due to the fact, that the voltage of d.c. supply source  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathrm{V_{CE}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0139em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">CE</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>  has zero resistance to an a.c. signal. An external resistor  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{R_E}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">E</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  is connected from the emitter to ground. The output of the circuit is taken across the resistor  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{R_E}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">E</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> .</p>
<p>It may be noted that in a common-collector transistor circuit, the input current is the base current  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathrm{I_B})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>  and the output current is the emitter current  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathrm{I_E})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">E</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> . Therefore, common-collector current gain is given</p>
<p>Transistors</p>
<p>by the relation,</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>γ</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msub><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></msub></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></msub><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>α</mi></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\gamma = \frac {I _ {\mathrm {E}}}{I _ {\mathrm {B}}} = \frac {I _ {\mathrm {E}}}{I _ {\mathrm {C}}} \times \frac {I _ {\mathrm {C}}}{I _ {\mathrm {B}}} = \frac {1}{\alpha} \times \beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em;
